Goal: To hold a razor blade properly for shaving.
Solution: Many people use a pinched grip like they are holding a pencil or throwing a dart. You have much more control if you hold razor in between the handle and razor. Getting behind the neck can be tricky and you may have to modify your grip.

Goal: How to clean a glass stovetop.
Solution: Pour white vinegar into a small spray bottle. Spray the vinegar evenly onto your stovetop.Then sprinkle baking soda evenly across your stovetop. The baking soda will react with the vinegar, creating a fizzy cleaner that will loosen up grease and grime.Next, put a few drops of Dawn into a bucket or your sink, and fill it with hot water.Dunk your towel into the soapy water, then wring it out lightly so that it’s wet but not dripping.Spread the wet towel over the stovetop, covering the baking soda and vinegar. Let it sit for about 15 minutes.Remove the towel and wipe away the remaining baking soda. To finish off, give your stovetop another spray with the vinegar, and use a microfiber cloth to buff it to a sparkling shine.

Goal: How to Clean Green Spot/Dust Algae off Aquarium Glass
Solution: Green spot or green dust algae is a common issue in planted tanks, because its common when there is an excess of nutrients and an excess of light in the tank. You can slow its growth by reducing fertilization, increasing water changes and reducing the intensity and duration of your lights. You'll probably also have to remove it manually, a good way to do it is to use a credit card and a magic eraser sponge, or an aquarium algae scraper tool. You can also keep Mystery or Nerite snails or otocinclus catfish are great algae eaters and good for peaceful, community tanks.

Goal: spicy fried rice
Solution: Brown 8 ounces diced andouille sausage in olive oil in a large skillet over medium-high heat; remove to a spoon. Goal: how do I make damper?
Solution: 2 cups self-raising flour    1 tablespoon sugar    1 tablespoon butter    1 cup milk extra for brushing    Instructions    Preheat oven to 180C.    Line a baking tray with baking paper.    In a large bowl, stir together flour, sugar and a generous pinch of salt.    Add the butter and rub in with your fingertips.    Add the milk and stir it in with a butter knife. The dough should be fairly soft, but not too sticky.    Turn out onto a lightly floured board and shape into a soft smooth ball.    Cut a cross shape into the top of the damper and brush with a little milk.    Bake for 30 minutes or until golden.

Goal: How to Make Huckleberry cobbler at home.
Solution: Wash  1 fresh or frozen wild huckleberry toss 1 berry with 3 tablespoons Lemon juice.  Use Pillsbury Cinnamon roll(tube type) from refrigerated section in the market, with rolling pin, roll to less than 1/2 inch thick.  Line the base of a deep metal baking pan/dish with the dough.  Reserve approx. 1/3 of dough for cover.  (You will place this on top after you finish preparing the filling.)  Place huckleberries in dish atop the roll dough.  Sprinkle 1 cup granulated sugar, 2 tbs. Brown sugar 1 tablespoons cinnamon, 1/2 cup butter (In small pieces), on top.  Sprinkle 1/2 tablespoon of salt atop.  Place crust over everything.  Bake in the oven at 375 for 40 min.  Remove from oven when crust brown and pie is bubbly.  Enjoy.

Goal: To bone a chicken thigh
Solution: Peel the skin off the chicken thigh using your fingers.Trim the excess yellow fat from the thigh with a paring knife. Flip over the thigh so that the rough side is up and locate the single bone that runs through it. Using the tip of the knife, score a line through the meat along the width of the bone. Expose the top of the bone by using the tip of your knife in short, flicking motions. Grasp one end of the bone with your non-knife hand (a little piece of paper towel can help if it's very slippery), then using the base of your knife, scrap the meat off of the bone in short, firm flicks. Separate the end of the bone completely from the meat. Trim away any gristle or bits of bone or cartilage that may have remained on the meat.

Goal: how do I find the Cygnus constellation
Solution: Cygnus the Swan is easy to find as it flies south and north along the path of the Milky Way. It is easiest to spot by looking straight up and looking for the three brightest stars forming what is known as the Summer Triangle. The bright star in the lower left of this triangle is Deneb, the tail of the swan.

Goal: How do you grow Roses?
Solution: Roses crave sun, at least six hours a day is ideal. Plant roses in rich, non-draining soil. When planting, mix organic matter, such as compost or ground bark, into excavated soil you'll use to backfill the planting hole. Add a 2-3-inch layer of coarse, organic mulch around roses. Coarse mulch helps reduce foliage diseases on roses because it reduces the amount of water splashing onto leaves (splashing water drops can spread fungal diseases).

Goal: How to make Rice Crisp Fantasy Fudge crunch at home.
Solution: Mix 3 cups granulated sugar,  3/4 cup margarine, and  2/3 cup evaporated milk in a large, heavy saucepan over medium heat, stirring to dissolve sugar. Bring mixture to a full boil for 5 minutes, stirring constantly.  Remove from heat and stir in 12 ounce semi sweet chocolate chips until melted and thoroughly combined. Beat in 1 7 ounce jar of marshmallow creme, 1 1/2 cup Rice Crispies, and 1 teaspoon vanilla extract.  Transfer fudge to Greased 8 x 13" pan and let cool before cutting into squares.

Goal: How to make vanilla pudding at home.
Solution: In a heavy saucepan 3/4 cup sugar and 3 tablespoons corn starch.  Stir in 3 cups milk.  Cook and stir over medium heat until bubbly.  Cook and stir 2 more min.  Remove from heat, gradually stir in 1 cup of the milk mixture in to 4 beaten egg yolks or 2 beaten eggs.  Add egg mixture to milk mixture, bring to gentle boil.  Cook and stir for 2 more min.  Remove from heat-  stir in 1 tablespoon butter and 1 1/2 teaspoons vanilla.  Pour into bowl cover with plastic wrap and chill, serve when set.

Goal: To make a spooky glowing jar for Halloween
Solution: Clean a mason jar using rubbing alcohol and a soft cloth. Completely cover the jar by wrapping it with masking tape. Draw a spooky jack-o'-lantern design on the tape with a Sharpie. Carefully cut along the design using a razor knife, and remove the rest of the tape. Spray the jar with black spray paint--you might need to use two coats depending on the kind of paint you use. After the paint dries, carefully remove the tape. Very very carefully, in an open, well ventilated space and wearing protective gloves, use the razor knife to cut the top from a glow stick and pour the liquid into the mason jar, and then fasten the lid. Carefully dispose of the empty glow stick. Swirl the liquid around the jar, and it should glow for up to two hours.

Goal: How to make Maple Nut Fantasy fudge at home.
Solution: Mix 3 cups granulated sugar,  3/4 cup margarine, and  2/3 cup evaporated milk in a large, heavy saucepan over medium heat, stirring to dissolve sugar. Bring mixture to a full boil for 5 minutes, stirring constantly.  Remove from heat and stir in 12 ounce bag of white chocolate chips until thoroughly combined. Beat in 1 7 ounce jar of marshmallow creme, 1/2 cup Maple syrup, and 1 teaspoon vanilla extract.  Transfer fudge to Greased 8 x 13" pan and let cool before cutting into squares.

Goal: How does companion planting help reduce pests and increase production ?
Solution: Like nature, combining different types of plants will help neighboring plants in a symbolic fashion, by adding colour, and scents and other things that can attract snails and slugs, also giving the wasps food so all can survive together. For instance. planting rosemary, lemon basil or wormwood on the edge of the fruit or vegetable garden will keep pests out as the wind carries the scent and oils across the garden. Beneficial plants add nectars that attract and feed insects, yarrow foliage composts the soil naturally.

Goal: To write on plastic
Solution: Write on plastic using a marker, and the marker will rub right off. Take the plastic surface you want to write upon, and run a small candle or chef's blowtorch back and forth across it. Move quickly, so it doesn't melt or get discolored. When the surface has cooled, use a marker to write on it. The surface will have oxidized, and the marker won't rub off!

Goal: How do you set up an aquarium for African Shell Dwelling Cichlids?
Solution: There several species of shell dwelling cichlids in the aquarium hobby. They are the smallest species of cichlids in the world, and they inhabit small empty snail shells at the bottom of Lake Tanganyika. To set up a tank for these little guys, you will want an aquarium of at least 20 gallons for a harem of 6 fish- 5 females and 1 male. These fish like harder water, so used crushed coral for the substrate as it ast like a buffer and raises the pH. Then you can buy Extra large escargot shells from a gourmet foods retailer, rinse them well, and sink them in the aquarium. Make sure your tank is completely cycled and add your fish.

Goal: How to Store Easy Homemade Butter in the refrigerator
Solution: To store Easy Homemade Butter in the refrigerator, take the lump of butter that remains in the bottom of the jar after you have poured off the buttermilk. Add a few inches of cold water, almost covering the butter in the bottom of the jar and shake again until the water looks cloudy. Pour this off and repeat, until the water after shaking remains clear. This will remove any further buttermilk so the butter doesn't spoil as quickly and can be stored in the refrigerator. Press out any remaining buttermilk and scrape the butter into a ball or bar shape. Wrap in parchment and store in the refrigerator.

Goal: Is there an easy way to make a sparkly pendant?
Solution: You'll need borax crystals, hot water, a pot to boil the water in, a spoon, a pipe cleaner, some string, a pencil or long stick, and food coloring. Boil 6 cups of water and mix in 3 cups of borax washing crystals. Add your preferred food color and mix. Take your pipe cleaner and shape it into a spiral, or any shape you like. Tie one end of your string around the pipe cleaner shape and the other end around a pencil or stick that is longer than the container of colored water. Dangle the pipe cleaner all the way down into the colored water, make sure it doesn't rest on the bottom. Leave it overnight, and when you pull your pipe cleaner shape out it will be covered in gobs of sparkly crystals that will glimmer in the light.

Goal: How to Identify Ich or Ick (Ichthyophthirius Multifilis) in Freshwater Fish
Solution: Ich is the most common fish illness in the freshwater aquarium hobby. Luckily, it is pretty easy to treat. The first step is positively identifying the parasitic infection. The infection looks like grains of white sand or salt all over the fishes fins, gills and eventually scales. The finnage may also appear tattered, and the fish may display flashing behavior, which looks like it is scratching its body on the substrate or ornaments to itch a scratch. Eventually, without treatment, as the infection progresses, the parasites attach themselves to the gills and the fish will settle at the bottom gasping, and eventually expire.

Goal: homemade sugar cookies
Solution: 3/4 cups (6oz/170g) butter, cubes and cold    1 cups (8oz/225g) sugar    2 eggs*    1 teaspoon vanilla extract    2 1/2 cups (12oz/340g) all-purpose flour    1 teaspoon baking powder    1 teaspoon salt    Instructions    In a food processor add in the flour, sugar, salt, and baking powder. Stir a little with a spatula        Add in the cold butter and blitz for seconds JUST until the mix looks like big bread crumbs    Whisk together the eggs and vanilla extract. Pour into the food processor and pulse for a few seconds until the dough comes together. Take care not to over mix. If your mix seems dry you can add a tiny bit more egg or milk.  (This dough can also be made by hand by rubbing in the butter into the flour)        Chill the dough for a minimum of 2-3 hours. Preferably chill overnight. Also it can be frozen at this stage for up to 8 weeks.         Once chilled, roll out some of the dough on a well floured surface to about 1/4-1/8 inch thick.         Cut out your desired shapes and transfer them to a baking tray lined with parchment. (this is a soft dough so work fast).    Bake at 325°F (160°C) for 18-20 minutes or until a light golden brown. Set aside to cool.        Decorate with royal icing if you wish and store in an airtight container for up to 7 days.

Goal: How to make Raspberry Pine nut fudge at home.
Solution: Mix 3 cups granulated sugar,  3/4 cup margarine, and  2/3 cup evaporated milk in a large, heavy saucepan over medium heat, stirring to dissolve sugar. Bring mixture to a full boil for 5 minutes, stirring constantly.  Remove from heat and stir in 12 ounce semi sweet chocolate chips until melted and thoroughly combined. Beat in 1 7 ounce jar of marshmallow creme, 3/4 cup dried Raspberries, 1/4 cup Pine nuts and 1 teaspoon vanilla extract. Transfer fudge to Greased 8 x 13" pan and let cool before cutting into squares.

Goal: How do you warm up a cold honeybee inside?
Solution: Carefully slide a stiff piece of paper underneath the bee to pick it up. Place the bee into a lidded container and cover it with saran wrap. Secure the saran wrap with a rubber band. Punch a few small holes into the saran wrap so the bee can get fresh air. Bring the container to a warm area indoors and give the bee time to warm up. Once the bee is active within the container, take the container outside, remove the saran wrap from the container, and release it.

Goal: How to make dulce de leche in an Instant Pot
Solution: Mix 1/2 teaspoon of baking soda with two tablespoons in water in a stainless steel bowl that will fit into the instant pot. Add one 300ml can of  condensed milk into the bowl with the baking soda mixture and mix with a whisk. Place the bowl into the Instant Pot and add one cup of water to the pot around it. Cook at high pressure for one hour, until the condensed milk mixture is deep brown. Carefully remove the bowl from the Instant Pot, and use a whisk to mix the cooked ingredients together. Pour into a clean glass jar and allow to cool.

Now, make a Prusik knot on your poles, pass the loop through the straps, and clip it onto a carabiner. Stake out the loose ends of the long line to secure the “tent”. Goal: How to make Apricot Cobbler at home.
Solution: Wash, peel and slice, 6 apricots  coat with 12 cups  Lemon Juice.  Use Pillsbury Cinnamon roll(tube type) from refrigerated section in the market, with rolling pin, roll to less than 1/2 inch thick.  Line the base of a deep metal baking pan/dish with the dough.  Reserve approx. 1/3 of dough for cover.  (You will place this on top after you finish preparing the filling.)  Place apricots in dish atop the roll dough.  Sprinkle 1 cup granulated sugar, 2 tbs. Brown sugar 1 tablespoons cinnamon, 1/2 cup butter (In small pieces), on top.  Sprinkle 1/2 tablespoon of salt atop.  Place crust over everything.  Bake in the oven at 375 for 40 min.  Remove from oven when crust brown and pie is bubbly.  Enjoy.

Goal: How to keep a toddler's toys organized
Solution: Children can accumulate so many toys that it is difficult to keep them organized. I separate toys into several different large tupperware bins and I store them in my bedroom closet. I take out one bin a week, so the child does not get bored of the toys, and there aren't so many available to choose from that the child gets overwhelmed. Then at the end of the week, I go through and throw away any brand new toys or toys missing pieces, put that box away, and exchange it for a different one.

When you release the leather it will have been embossed.

Goal: To make an All-American grilled cheese
Solution: Preheat a heavy cast iron skillet on medium heat on the stove-top. Spread room temperature butter onto a slice of bread and place the buttered side down on the skillet. Goal: Bake a holiday Cranberry/apple cobbler at home.
Solution: Peel and core 2 large or  3 medium apples (tart ones are best), Wash 2 cups fresh cranberries add with apples.  Slice the apple thinly, sprinkle with 1/4 cup Lemon Juice.  Use Pillsbury Cinnamon roll(tube type) from refrigerated section in the market, with rolling pin, roll to less than 1/2 inch thick.  Line the base of a deep metal baking pan/dish with the dough.  Reserve approx. 1/3 of dough for cover.  (You will place this on top after you finish preparing the filling.)  Place apples and cranberries in dish atop the roll dough.  Sprinkle 1 cup granulated sugar, 2 tbs. Brown sugar 2 tablespoons cinnamon, 1/2 cup butter (In small pieces), on top.  Sprinkle 1/2  pounds of salt atop.  Place crust over everything.  Bake in the oven at 375 for 40 min.  Remove from oven when crust brown and pie is bubbly.  Enjoy.

Goal: How do you make a juicer out of a can to juice berries with?
Solution: Empty out a soup can and clean it. Get a 1 inch long nail and a hammer. Flip the can upside down and place the nail tip down on the center of the bottom of the can. Hold the nail steady with one hand and raise the hammer above the nail with the other hand. Swiftly swing the hammer down face-first onto the top of the nail, pushing it through the bottom of the can. Pull the nail out and repeat about 150-200 times, until there are many small holes in the bottom of the can.

Goal: To change a broken capacitor,
Solution: use a heating pen to heat the capacitor until it is completely burnt. Once it has turned to ashes, you are free to add a new capacitor in its place and solder it to the PCB so it stays in place.
